src="http://web.archive.org/web/20191030205145im_/http://a.espncdn.com/combiner/i/?img=/photo/2017/0201/r177066_1296x729_16-9.jpg&amp;w=738&amp;site=espnfc" width="738"/>\n<figcaption>Hiroshi Kiyotake made 10 starts for Sevilla in all competitions.</figcaption></figure>\n<p>Sevilla have announced the sale of midfielder Hiroshi Kiyotake to his former club Cerezo Osaka.</p>\n<p>Kiyotake, 27, joined Sevilla from Hannover last summer but has struggled for playing time this campaign, making four La Liga appearances.</p>\n<p>The Japan international now returns to his ex-side Cerezo Osaka, who he left in 2012 for a move to Nurnberg.</p>\n<p></p>\n<blockquote class="twitter-tweet" data-lang="en">\n<p dir="ltr" lang="sl">TRANSFER | <a href="http://web.archive.org/web/20191030205145/https://t.co/9Dh8tjFeDW">pic.twitter.com/9Dh8tjFeDW</a></p>\n- Sevilla FC (@SevillaFC_ENG) <a href="http://web.archive.org/web/20191030205145/https://twitter.com/SevillaFC_ENG/status/826734750517846017">February 1, 2017</a></blockquote>\n<p>Sevilla sporting director Monchi said of Kiyotake: "With him, it was not just about playing, he also left because of personal reasons.</p>\n<p>"We have defended the club\'s interests but we are also mindful of the player as a person."</p>\n<p><i>Follow @ESPNFC on Twitter to keep up with the latest football updates.\n\n\n\n</i></p><div class="article-util"><div class="sponsored-links"><div {'_id': ObjectId('605b8d177655c2d7f90c8c91'), 'url': 'http://comm.uoregon.edu/newsreleases/2004/20040430B.html', 'hostname': 'uoregon.edu', 'title': '<html>\n<head>\n\n\n\n\n\n<!-- End Wayback Rewrite JS Include -->\n<title>University of Oregon News Releases</title>\n<script language="javascript" src="http://localhost:24680/domdistiller.js" type="text/javascript"></script></head>\n<body alink="#00FF00" bgcolor="#ffffff" link="#008000" vlink="#008000">\n<b><font face="Melior" size="4">\n<p align="CENTER">UO HONORS OREGON MUTUAL FUND INNOVATOR JAMES RIPPEY</p>\n</font></b>\n<p>April 30, 2004</p>\n<p>Contact Pauline Austin, (541) 346-3129, <a href="http://web.archive.org/web/20060903062014/mailto:paustin@uoregon.edu">paustin@uoregon.edu</a></p>\n<br/><br/>\n<dir></dir>\n<p>EUGENE\x97James Rippey, a Portland businessman whose company established Oregon\x92s first mutual fund, will be recognized for his business and community leadership with the 2004 University of Oregon Pioneer Award.</p>\n<p>The 1953 UO business graduate will be honored during a gala event on Friday, May 7, at the Portland Hilton.</p>\n<p>Rippey, who grew up in Coos Bay, Ore., and his colleague, J. Jerry Inskeep Jr., formed their own investment management firm, Columbia Management Co. The company established the Columbia Growth Fund, Oregon\x92s first mutual fund, in 1967, and the Columbia Daily Co., one of the first money-market mutual funds in the country, in 1974. During Rippey\x92s tenure, the company grew its management portfolio to $22 billion. In 1997, the firm was acquired by Fleet Financial Group of Boston, Mass.</p>\n<p>"Jim Rippey has been a remarkable trailblazer, transforming Oregon\x92s investment industry and, through his extremely generous philanthropy, transforming the lives of the citizens of Oregon," said UO President Dave Frohnmayer.</p>\n<p>In addition to his guidance of Columbia, Rippey has held leadership roles in the Providence St. Vincent Hospital and Medical Center Foundation, the Portland Rotary Charitable Trust and the University of Oregon Foundation.</p>\n<p>Inaugurated in 1979, the UO Pioneer Award is presented to alumni and others who have become leaders and risk-takers in their fields. Last year\x92s award went to Ann Curry \x9178, news anchor on the NBC "Today Show." Other past winners include Nike co-founder Phil Knight \x9259; Emery Barnes \x9254, the first black speaker of the British Columbia legislative assembly; and acclaimed film director James Ivory \x9251.</p>\n<p>Net proceeds from the black-tie event will go to the Pioneer Award Presidential Scholarship, and those who wish can contribute to the scholarship fund even if they don\x92t attend. For information, call the Special Events Office in the UO Office of Development, (541) 346-0783.</p>\n<p>For more information, go to <a href="http://web.archive.org/web/20060903062014/http://duckhenge.uoregon.edu/hparchive/display.php?q=rippeypioneeraward.html">http://duckhenge.uoregon.edu/hparchive/display.php?q=rippeypioneeraward.html</a>.</p>\n<p align="CENTER">\x9730\x97</p>\n<p><font size="1">#B-6170/Local,OrDailies,PDX,ORBUS</font></p>\n</body>\n</html><!--\n     FILE ARCHIVED ON 06:20:14 Sep 03, 2006 AND RETRIEVED FROM THE\n     INTERNET ARCHIVE ON 19:06:47 Mar 24, 2021.\n     JAVASCRIPT APPENDED BY WAYBACK MACHINE, COPYRIGHT INTERNET ARCHIVE.\n\n     ALL OTHER CONTENT MAY ALSO BE PROTECTED BY COPYRIGHT (17 U.S.C.\n     SECTION 108(a)(3)).\n-->\n<!--\nplayback timings (ms):\n  captures_list: 173.655\n  exclusion.robots: 0.089\n  exclusion.robots.policy: 0.083\n  RedisCDXSource: 11.862\n  esindex: 0.007\n  LoadShardBlock: 143.585 (3)\n  PetaboxLoader3.datanode: 146.483 (4)\n  CDXLines.iter: 16.381 (3)\n  load_resource: 814.777\n  PetaboxLoader3.resolve: 721.554\n-->'}
